## Purpose

This file is the authoritative final-draft version of `f079r`.

  Operational English: Circulate the charge, then clamp and test the flow, then let the fraction settle, keeping the line aligned with modular cell choreography self contained micro rituals synchronized into a.

- `P.1`

### Hacking Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[\pi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \pi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^- \oplus e_{\mathrm{P_1}}, \qquad e_{\mathrm{P_1}} \in E_{\mathrm{safe}} \iff \mathrm{seal}(e_{\mathrm{P_1}})=1 \land \mathrm{budget}(e_{\mathrm{P_1}})\le B_{\mathrm{P_1}}\]

  Variable legend: `pi` is the route, `e_line` the next admissible edge, `B_line` the seal budget.
  Reading: settle phase / volatile outlet / fluid conduit line.

### Game Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: settle phase / volatile outlet / fluid conduit line.
  Confidence: strong

- `P.10`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_10}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_10}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_10}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_10}}^-)\}\]

  Confidence: strong

## Direct Operational Meaning

A modular instruction lattice: each cluster is a self-contained micro-ritual (cycle → clamp → commit), and the full page is the stitched choreography that synchronizes many bath-cells into one coherent system. Process statistics: 77 circulation commands (qo-); 15 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 21 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 3 completion markers (daiin).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f79r` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=55, N_valve=6, and N_seal=3. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f79r` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.

## All-Lens Zero Point

`A modular instruction lattice: each cluster is a self-contained micro-ritual (cycle → clamp → commit), and the full page is the stitched choreography that synchronizes many bath-cells into one coherent system.`

\[g = \mathrm{Coll}(X), \qquad X = \mathrm{Expand}(g) \oplus r\]

### Typed State Machine

\[
\mathcal R_{f79r} = \{r_{charge}, r_{circulate}, r_{clamp}, r_{commit}, r_{seal}\}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{charge})=r_{circulate}, \qquad
\delta(r_{circulate})=r_{clamp}, \qquad
\delta(r_{clamp})=
\begin{cases}
r_{circulate} & \text{if } \Delta_n > 0 \\
r_{commit} & \text{if } \Delta_n = 0
\end{cases}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{commit})=
\begin{cases}
r_{seal} & \text{if } P_{salt} = 1 \\
r_{circulate} & \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
\]
